<S n="1500">
<s>kaH kasya puruzo banDuH kimApyaM kasya kenacit .</s>
<s>eko hi jAyate jantureka eva vinaSyati ..</s>
</S>
<S n="1501">
<s>tasmAnmAtA pitA ceti rAma sajjeta yo naraH .</s>
<s>unmatta iva sa jYeyo nAsti kaScidDi kasyacit ..</s>
</S>
<D n="1500" a="3859">
<b>1500.</b> (<b>3859.</b>) Wer ist des Andern
Angehöriger? Was kann Einer durch den
Andern erlangen? Allein kommt ja der
Mensch zur Welt und allein scheidet er
von ihr.
</D>
<D n="1501" a="3860">
<b>1501.</b> (<b>3860.</b>) Darum ist, o Rāma, der
Mann, der sich an Jemanden klammert,
weil dieser seine Mutter oder sein Vater
ist, für verrückt zu halten: Niemand
gehört ja einem Andern. <pb n="1.288"/>
</D>
<F n="1500,1">
1500.1) R. ed. Bomb. und SCHL. 2,
108, 3. 4. ed. GORR. 116, 12. fg. 1500,
²b. <s>kiM kAryaM</s> st. <s>kimApyaM</s>
GORR. ²c. <s>yadeko</s> st. <s>eko hi</s>
SCHL. und GORR. ²c. <s>yadeko</s> st. <s>eko
hi</s> SCHL. und GORR. 1501, ²a. ²b.
<s>cEva pratiSrayasamAvuBO</s> GORR. ²c.
²d. <s>iva vijYeyo yo'tra sajjeta vE
naraH</s> GORR.
</F>

<D n="1505" a="585">
<b>1505.</b> (<b>585.</b>) Hartherzige, lass den auf
falschen Berichten beruhenden Irrthum
fahren! Auf die Worte von Hinterbringern
hin darfst du mich nicht in Schmerz
versetzen! Oder hältst du etwa, o
Einfältige, dieses wirklich für
Wahrheit? Nun dann thue an mir, o
Geliebte, was dir gut dünkt und gehabe
dich wohl!
</D>

<S n="1512">

<D n="1512" a="588">
<b>1512.</b> (<b>588.</b>) Kaum hatte ich nach der
Rückkehr des Geliebten, der in seinen
Antworten sich verwirrte, abgezehrt
durch die Trennung, verstellter Weise
diese Thränen vergossen, als ich wieder
im leeren Gemache tief aufseufzte:
dieses wurde ich gewahr, als ich die
Augen unruhig umhergehen liess, da ich
vorher nicht bedacht hatte, dass mein
Weinen zu den Ohren der strengen
Freundin gelangen könnte.
</D>

<S n="1514">

<S n="1515">
<s>satyenotpadyate Darmo dayAdAnErvivarDate .</s>
<s>kzamayA sTApyate DarmaH kroDaloBErvinaSyati ..</s>
</S>
<D n="1514">
<b>1514.</b> Woraus entspringt moralisches
Verdienst? Wodurch wächst moralisches
Verdienst? Wodurch wird moralisches
Verdienst befestigt? Wodurch schwindet
moralisches Verdienst?
</D>
<D n="1515">
<b>1515.</b> Aus der Wahrhaftigkeit
entspringt moralisches Verdienst; durch
Mitleid und Spenden wächst moralisches
Verdienst; durch Nachsicht wird
moralisches Verdienst befestigt; durch
Zorn und Habsucht schwindet moralische
Verdienst.
</D>
<F n="1514,15">
1514.15) SUBHĀṢ. 162. 1514, ²a.

<entry>
<info L="1724" page="1.332" gtypes="S,D,F,V3"/>
<S n="1724">
<s>kiM syAdvarRacatuzwayena vanajaM varREstriBirBUzaRaM</s>
<s>syAdAdyena mahI trayeRa ca PalaM maDyadvaye prARadam .</s>
<s>vyaste gotraturaMgaGAsakusumaM prAnte ca saMboDanaM</s>
<s>ye jAnanti buDottamAH kzititale tezAmahaM kiMkaraH ..</s>
</S>
<D n="1724">
<b>1724.</b> Was mag mit seinen vier Silben
eine blaue Wasserlilie sein, mit dreien
ein Schmuck, mit der ersten die Erde,
wieder mit dreien eine Frucht, mit den
zwei mittleren Leben verleihend, mit
versetzten Silben Familie, Pferdefutter
und Blume, mit der Schlusssilbe ein
Vocativ? Wer von den klügsten Männern
auf Erden dieses wissen sollte, dessen
Diener will ich sein. (<s>kuvalaya,
valaya, ku, kuvala, vala</s> d. i. <s>bala,
kula, yava, vakula</s> d. i. <s>bakula,
kuvalaya</s>).
</D>
<F n="1724">
1724) SUBHĀṢ. 283. ²d. <s>nezAm</s> st.
<s>tezAm</s> die Hdschr.
</F>
<V3 n="1724">
1724. ²c. WEBER ist mit meiner
Auffassung von <s>prAnte ca saMboDanam</s>
nicht einverstanden und äussert sich im
Literarischen Centralblatt 1872, No. 31,
Sp. 839. fg. hierüber folgendermaassen:
«Die Worte <s>prAnte ca saMboDanam</s>
bedeuten schwerlich: «was mag … mit der
Schlusssilbe ein Vocativ sein?» was gar
keinen fasslichen Sinn giebt, sondern
beziehen sich auf das <s>aye</s> und <s>ayi
saMboDane</s> der Lexicographen und sind
zu übersetzen: «was dient in dem
Schlusse als Partikel des Anrufs?» Auf
die verschiedene Vocalisirung in diesem
letzteren Falle kommt es eben so wenig
an, wie unsere Rebus und Worträthsel es
mit der Orthographie genau zu nehmen
pflegen». Da der Dichter bis dahin stets
nur mit Silben im indischen Sinne
gespielt hat, glaube ich nicht, dass er
unter <s>prAnta</s> etwas Anderes verstehen
sollte, als wiederum eine Silbe. Aber
hätte er auch mit einzelnen Lauten
gespielt, was ja sonst geschieht
(WEBER verweist auf
KĀVYĀD. 3, 114), so würde er nach
meinem Dafürhalten auch dann die drei
letzten Laute nicht schlechtweg als
<s>prAnta</s> zusammengefasst haben. Und
nun merke man wohl, dass WEBER noch
weiter geht, indem er nicht etwa genau
diese verstanden haben will, sondern den
Schlussvocal ohne Weiteres ändert,
obgleich er keinen Beleg dafür hat, dass
die Inder in ihren Räthseln je in dieser
Weise verführen. Bei meiner Auffassung
soll <s>prAnte ca saMboDanam</s> keine
Eigenthümlichkeit des Wortes
<s>kuvalaya</s> hervorheben, sondern nur
die Auffindung des gesuchten Wortes
erleichtern, indem durch diesen Zusatz
ziemlich deutlich zu verstehen gegeben
wird, dass das Wort ein auf <s>a</s>
ausgehendes Thema sei. Bei dieser
Gelegenheit will ich bemerken, dass in
den Nachträgen im Wörterbuch unter
<s>ekavarRaka</s> die angesetzte Bedeutung
zu streichen und st. dessen «einsilbig»
zu setzen ist. Die Cäsur ist nämlich
unsatthaft, wenn die beiden Theile des
Wortes einsilbig sind d. i. in einem
zweisilbigen Worte.
</V3>
</entry>

man ausschliesslich (oder in der
Einsamkeit) denken? An Viṣṇu's
Füssepaar. Was soll man sich angelegen
sein lassen? Das Gute. An Viṣṇu's
Füssepaar. Was soll man sich angelegen
sein lassen? Das Gute. Wonach soll man
Verlangen tragen? Nach Mitleid. Giebt
sich das Herz diesen hin, so kann es der
unbegrenzten Erlösung theilhaftig
werden.
</D>
<F n="1769">
1769) KĀVYAPR. 170. Vgl. den vorangehenden Spruch.

<S n="1814">

</S>
<D n="1814">
<b>1814.</b> Wer sich anstrengt, dem gelingt
es, o Yudhiṣṭhira, hier auf Erden in
der Regel; der Träge dagegen erlebt
nimmer die vollkommene Reife der Frucht.
</D>
<F n="1814">

<entry>
<info L="1815" page="1.351" gtypes="S,D,F"/>
<S n="1815">
<s>kurvanti tAvatpraTamaM priyARi yAvanna jAnanti naraM prasaktam .</s>
<s>jYAtvATa taM manmaTapASabadDaM grastAmizaM mInamivodDaranti ..</s>
</S>
<D n="1815" a="699">
<b>1815.</b> (<b>699.</b>) Die Weiber thun zuerst
freundlich, aber nur so lange, als sie
sehen, dass der Mann ihnen noch nicht
anhängt; sehen sie den Mann mit der
Liebe Banden gefesselt, dann ziehen sie
ihn wie einen Fisch, der den Köder
verschluckt hat, hinauf an die Luft.
</D>
<F n="1815">
1815) PAÑCAT. ed. KOSEG. I, 208. ed.
Bomb. 193. ²c. <s>ca</s> st. <s>aTa</s>

<D n="1999">
<b>1999.</b> Welche Entfernung besteht nicht
zwischen der Mondscheibe und dem Meere,
zwischen der Sonne und einem Teich mit
Tagwasserrosen, zwischen einer
Wolkenmasse und einem Trupp Pfauen,
zwischen einer Biene und einer
Jasminstaude, zwischen einem
unvergleichlich schönen Schwarme in
weite Ferne gezogener Flamingos und dem
klaren See Mānasa! Was man in Folge
vorangegangener Werke lieb hat, das
bleibt Einem lieb trotz aller Entferung.
</D>
